  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText10589373654910538600" style="display:none">Down in Atlanta, tempers – and temperatures – are about to flare…<br /><br />As a mercenary who cleans up after magic gone wrong, Kate Daniels has seen her share of occupational hazards. Normally, waves of paranormal energy ebb and flow across Atlanta like a tide. But once every seven years, a flare comes, a time when magic runs rampant. Now Kate’s going to have to deal with problems on a much bigger scale: a divine one.<br /><br />When Kate sets out to retrieve a set of stolen maps for the Pack, Atlanta’s paramilitary clan of shapeshifters, she quickly realizes much more at stake. During a flare, gods and goddesses can manifest – and battle for power. The stolen maps are only the opening gambit in an epic tug-of-war between two gods hoping for rebirth. And if Kate can’t stop the cataclysmic showdown, the city may not survive…</span>

  <span id="freeText12335249925830178273" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380369478i/722244.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Hmmm I wonder what this Magic Burns book will be about</i><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380369478i/722245.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>What?? I mean.. What?? This can’t be right</i><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380369478i/722245.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Why isn’t she being stupid?? AM-I-RITE???<br><br>One thing I love about Ilona Andrews is the fact that she didn’t make Kate a sappy character. Not once did she have a "love" thought about any of the hot dudes in the book. Not once. Sure, she thinks about banging them but that’s the normal thing to do. No unnecessary crap about love at first sight and all that shit means a happier me. Plus her relationship with Curran is so good. I’m enjoying every minute of it. And you know what? They’ll be together in the future (DUH) so seeing how they develop their relationship is so much fun. It’s almost as good as playing Sims 3. But Sims 3 is way better because it makes you god. Being god beats everything else. So nah, close but not close enough!<br><br> Speaking of which, wasn’t Ghastek awesome? He’s taking RPG games to the next level. How cool would it be to be able to control your game character in real life? That would be so fucking awesome! What would I do with it? Conquer Earth, of course. Kill everyone who pisses me off. Spy on people. Lurk in dark alleys and scare the shit out of anyone who walks by. And loot everything. I’m the looting type so can’t help myself, sistah!<br><br>But back to Kate. I love Kate. I love Kate so much my heart hurts. I love Kate so much I started writing poems just for her. I love Kate so much I started baking cakes for her each morning. <br><br>Yes Kate, go samurai on their sorry asses! Yes Kate, give them the middle finger!! Yes Kate, ride your horse into the sunset!!! Yes Kate, spank me one more time!!!!!!<br><br>Wait. What?</span>

<div id="review_351650230" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/351650230" />
    <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow"><img alt="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393785730p2/10336538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/351650230?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow">Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/8166133-magic-burns">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">The WHOLE world.</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=skulduggery">skulduggery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=i-cried">i-cried</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=kickass-heroines">kickass-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=buddy-reads-are-the-best">buddy-reads-are-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=weres-shapeshifters">weres-shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=dead-things">dead-things</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=creeptastic">creeptastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer351650230" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9946226940270548822"><b>5/6/18:</b> I hope that when the Andrews write their Julie and Derek spinoff that one of the books takes place during another flare and Red shows up. Then I want for Julie and/or Derek to break several of his bones. Big important ones. Like a femur and his pelvis. Yeah. <br/><br/><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>After the trial by fire world-building of MAGIC BITES, any leftover questions are quickly answered in KATE DANIELS #2 by virtue of the shifts from magic to tech and tech to magic occurring with alarming frequency as a result</span>
  <span id="freeText9946226940270548822" style="display:none"><b>5/6/18:</b> I hope that when the Andrews write their Julie and Derek spinoff that one of the books takes place during another flare and Red shows up. Then I want for Julie and/or Derek to break several of his bones. Big important ones. Like a femur and his pelvis. Yeah. <br><br><b>4.5 stars</b><br><br>After the trial by fire world-building of MAGIC BITES, any leftover questions are quickly answered in KATE DANIELS #2 by virtue of the shifts from magic to tech and tech to magic occurring with alarming frequency as a result of one of this book's Big Problems, the magical Flare.<br><br>SIDENOTE: that's "Flare" as in flare-up, not "flair" as in you need at least 15 pieces on your uniform. FYI.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387492497ra/7606558.gif" width="349" height="199" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Right. SO a magic Flare has happened every 7(ish) years since tech fell, and during a Flare, not only are the magic/tech shifts more frequent, but the magic is more POTENT. <br><br>More strange things happen, more creatures show up, already existing magical people and creatures have a harder time maintaining control over their magical aspects.&lt;------it's a MESS.<br><br>The Casino, the headquarters of The People, shuts down entirely, going into lockdown. <br><br>But I'm getting ahead of myself.<br><br>MAGIC BURNS begins with Kate getting an early morning wakeup call from Jim, who needs backup on a Mercenary Guild gig. About the time they've got everything wrapped-up, Jim gets a mysterious text, and ditches Kate, b/c "Pack business." Kate is understandably annoyed. She's only one person, and hardly capable of carrying BOTH the dead (shot in the back with an arrow by person(s) unknown) perp <i>and</i> the salamander contained by magical glass, and they only get paid if they have proof they took care of the problem.<br><br>So what does Kate do?<br><br>She cuts off Perp's head. So pragmatic, our Kate.<br><br>After dumping the head and the fire lizard at the Guild, Kate moseys over to the Order, where Derek asks for her help on behalf of the Pack. <br><br>A group of surveyors was ambushed, you see, by a man who stole their maps and <i>literally</i> disappeared. This mysterious man left behind several arrows matching the one that killed Perp, so Kate heads back to the parking deck where she cornered Perp that morning, and looks for a clue. (&lt;------I LOVE it when Kate looks for clues.)<br><br>What she finds is a creepy magnetized metal yard with Stymphalian birds, what looks like a smashed air hanger with a bottomless pit underneath where a cauldron used to sit, and two street kids.<br><br>One of those street kids is Julie (Yay!!). The other street kid is Red (boo hiss).<br><br>Also in the weird, smushed air hanger is a bizarre skeleton pinned to some crates by more familiar looking arrows. Kate decides to investigate, removes an arrow or two, and what-do-you-know, the bowman somehow knows and comes to investigate. <br><br>The bowman's name is Bran, and Bran is HOT. He's mischievous and has swagger and I LOVE him.<br><br>After lots of flirty banter (and maybe a scuffle or two), Bran gives Kate the maps and . . . disappears.<br><br>Red is long gone by this point, so Kate takes Julie under her wing, stuff happens, Curran in his Alpha-ness is even more HOT than Bran, Kate is even more KICK-ASS than we previously thought, and this second installment pretty much kills the first one (and the first book was PRE-tty dang good IMO). <br><br>This is a series that just keeps getting better, and if you haven't checked it out yet . . . you NEED to check it out. Anyone who loves or is interested in Urban Fantasy should have KATE DANIELS in their library. Come on . . . time to drink the kool-aid. This won't hurt a bit, I promise. *orbit gum smile*<br><br><b>My other reviews for this series:</b><br><br><b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2136352204" rel="nofollow noopener">A Questionable Client (Kate Daniels, #0.5)</a>

 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>Original review</b>]<br><br><i>☆☆☆ Post-Shift Productions proudly present ☆☆☆</i><br><b>Just Another Day in the Life of Kate Daniels</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422176678i/13467151.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>►<b>2.00 a.m.:</b> enjoying a good night's sleep. Phone rings. <i>Jim here! Rise and shine Kate! Time to go kill things!</i> <b>Here we go again</b>.<br>► <b>3.00 a.m.:</b> how to carry a dead, homicidal pyromaniac and a salamander in an enchanted sphere at the same time? Easy. <b>Decapitation will do the trick every time</b>. <br>► <b>4.00 a.m.:</b> Spend hours at the Guild filling in paperwork. <i>State the suspect’s intent as perceived by you: intended to burn down the city due to being a complete crackpot.</i> <b>There, that should do it</b>.<br>► <b>8.00 a.m.:</b> visit from Curran's significant other. She needs a personal favour. <b>This is going to be one of those days is it?</b><br>► <b>8.30 a.m.:</b> visit from your <b>teenage werewolf sidekick</b> aka Boy Wonder. Get lectured about your would have been boyfriend. Learn about a <b>supernaturally fast sniper</b> who goes poof. The Pack needs your help. His Furry Highness requires your presence. <b>It's definitely one of those days</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431539165i/14845108.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>9.00 a.m.:</b> oh look! <b>A sexy man in a kilt!</b> He teleports! He regenarates! He talks zippers! Your hormones are overloading! <b>You need to get laid</b>.<br>► <b>9.30 a.m.:</b> meet Julie. Her <b>mom disappeared</b>. Go look for her. Find an <b>oversized metal hedgehog</b> instead. Oh was that your dog, you scumbag? So sorry about that. Lesson #1: pissing Kate Daniels off may result in <b>permanent damage to your freaky puppy</b>. <br>► <b>10.00 a.m.:</b> take Julie home. <b>Oh look, a friendly visitor</b>: female creature, long hair, claws, toxic goo. <i>Choke on your hair, you piece of crap.</i> Oh look, another one! <i><b>Get out of my house, you crazy bitch</b>.</i> Oh look, these lovely ladies brought a hooded friend along: eyes of a squid, green tentacles, hovers. <b>Cool</b>. <i>Amehe. Obey you sonofabitch</i>. <b>Oops. Blackout time</b>.<br>► <b>10.30 a.m.:</b> rescued by His Furriness. Oh, the irony. <i>You’re a fucking mess and you look like shit. <b>Thanks Your Majesty, I try</b>. </i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431596977i/14852449.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>11.00 a.m.:</b> at the Pack's Southeast office. Trying to recover. The Beast Lord himself pays you a visit. <b>Hands you a bowl of soup</b>. Discusses your underwear choices (no, you do not have barbed wire and a steal chain on your panties). <b>Mayday mayday</b>.<br>► <b>11.30 a.m.:</b> feeling much better. Go outside to get some fresh air. Curran flexing. Your hormones overloading. Again. <b>You <u>really</u> need to get laid</b>.<br>► <b>12.00 p.m.:</b> hey, Bran The Hero is back! Bust his nose again. <i>Love that bow on your panties dove.</i> Hit him with a chair. Get kissed. <b>The Beast Lord is not pleased</b>. <br>► <b>12.30 p.m.:</b> go on a field trip with Boy Wonder and Ghastek The Whole Puncher. <b>End up dancing with a very naked</b>, Roman statue-like Saiman in the snow. Feel something getting hard down there. <b>What did you ever do to anybody?</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431592984i/14852176.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>1.00 p.m.:</b> head off to meet the Oracle. Meet a Medusa impersonator. Sigh. Couldn't you run into a <b>colony of fluffy bunnies</b> for a change?<br>► <b>1.30 p.m.:</b> enter a living, giant tortoise through its mouth. <b>This is getting too weird, even for you</b>. <br>► <b>2.00 p.m.:</b> finally time to sit down and grab a bite to eat. <b>Chicken wings. Mmmm, pure bliss</b>. Wait. What's that? Only a gang of poisonous, maniacal reeves and their freakish shepherd. <b>Oh, good.</b> They brought a friend along, too. Kate, meet <s>Bubba</s> Ugad, the Great Crow's Hammer. <b>You're kidding right? Please tell me you're kidding.</b> <br>► <b>2.30 p.m.:</b> hey Bubba, nice tattoos you have there! <b>Whoa,</b> word of power alert! <b><i>Osanda</i>. Kneel</b>. Cut, cut, cut. Slice, slice, slice. <b>Buh bye Bubba</b>. <br>► <b>3.00 p.m.:</b> escape the city to pay the hyena pack a visit. Lovely <i>brood of social deviants with a penchant for <b>hysterical laughter and kinky sex</b>.</i> Yay.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431594531i/14852299._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>3.30 p.m.:</b> have an enlightening conversation with Aunt B about big furry cats and soup. <b>You need a drink</b>.<br>► <b>4.00 p.m.:</b> head to the Keep. Curran + magic flare = Fabio hair and powder keg with a short fuse. <b>Play cat and mouse</b>. <i>Osanda,</i> your Furry Highness. Not working? <i>Wedding,</i> your Furry Highness. <b>Ha! Got you there!</b> <br>► <b>4.30 p.m.:</b> well isn't that Mr Hey Dove <u>again</u>?! Oops, it looks like he just stole the survey maps <u>again</u>. <b>Err, is that thunder you hear?</b> No, just His Furriness roaring.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431596006i/14852384.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>5.00 p.m.:</b> shifters party time. Claws out. Rip some flesh. Kick some ass. <b>Fun times</b>. Meet a new friend: horse skull, double row of oversized teeth, Neanderthall eyebrows, cartilage breaking through skin. <b>Lovely look you have there</b>. <br>► <b>5.30 p.m.:</b> His Fussiness plans to hog-tie you, gag you and have 3 shifters sit on you. <b>Kinky</b>.<br>► <b>6.00 p.m.:</b> emulate daddy dearest and lead the furry army into battle. <b>No-Code day for the Pack</b>. Yay! Blood and gore await! Kneel, you undead mermaid bitches. Slice, slice, slice. Cut, cut, cut. Kill, kill, kill. <b>Best party ever</b>.<br>► <b>6.30 p.m.:</b> Ouch, that really hurt. <b>Die a little</b>. Oh look, a big cat! Gotta get to Julie. <b>Oh Bran</b>.<br>► <b>7.00 p.m.:</b> home at last. The door is open. <b>Strange</b>. The light is on. <b>Weird</b>. Smells like coffee. <b>What the hell?</b> Curran. The Princess Bride. <i>As you wish. <b>Psych</b>.</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422119861i/13458929.png" <span id="freeTextContainer1914174583589501095">Sexually frustrated Kate Daniels is being pursued by every interesting male creature in this book:<br/><br/>a)	Saiman (With a magic store body, a Polymorph i.e. he changes human forms): <br/><i>
  <b>“Can you dance? Dance with me Kate!”, <br/>“Stay with me. It will be fun.”</b>
</i><br/><br/>b)	Ghastec (One of the People, a Master of the Dead i.e. he creates vampires)<br/><b>
  <i>“A pleasure to see you, as always”, <br/>“You are in an excellent physical shape and you are well proportioned.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>c)	Bran (A goddess' hound, a scoundrel, a thief, a brigand, a h</span>
  <span id="freeText1914174583589501095" style="display:none">Sexually frustrated Kate Daniels is being pursued by every interesting male creature in this book:<br /><br />a)	Saiman (With a magic store body, a Polymorph i.e. he changes human forms): <br /><i>
  <b>“Can you dance? Dance with me Kate!”, <br />“Stay with me. It will be fun.”</b>
</i><br /><br />b)	Ghastec (One of the People, a Master of the Dead i.e. he creates vampires)<br /><b>
  <i>“A pleasure to see you, as always”, <br />“You are in an excellent physical shape and you are well proportioned.”</i>
</b><br /><br />c)	Bran (A goddess' hound, a scoundrel, a thief, a brigand, a human previously who just wanted to be hero and to be remembered)<br /><i>
  <b>“Keep me warm tonight and maybe I’ll feel generous in the morning.”<br />“Why don’t you sleep with me? Kiss me and I promise I’ll talk.”</b>
</i><br /><br />d)	Raphael (a fun, patient hyena, a male Bouda)<br /><b>
  <i>“Two years? That’s entirely too long. If you want, we can take care of that. After two years, it’s pure therapy.”</i>
</b><br /><br />And undoubtedly the absolute winner<br /><br />e)	Curran (The Furry Highness, the Lord of the Beasts, the Shapeshifters' Pack leader)<br /><b>
  <i>“Not only will you sleep with me, but you will say 'please.'<br />You will say 'please' before and 'thank you' after."</i>
</b><br /><br />Of course she is not saving herself for marriage. <br />The reasons are more complicated and involve the exchange of magic and great power.<br /><br />Oh and there was some fighting all around in the book, but I was not paying attention.<br /><br />(Okay, I am only joking. The battles were magnificent!)</span>
  <a data-text-id="1914174583589501095" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1175318775" />
    <a title="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8734459-tadiana-night-owl"><img alt="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603085284p2/8734459.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1175318775?book_show_action=true">Jan 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=you-go-girl-kickass-heroine">you-go-girl-kickass-heroine</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1175318775" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17474147930571051738">April 2018 update: After holding out for two years, I finally renewed my $70 nonresident library card. I was so stoked when I found that the library now has the entire Kate Daniels series! I brought The. Entire. Series. home with me, and I’m starting with this one and working my way through the series, since there are a few I’ve never read. Cheer me on!<br/><br/>This second book in the Kate Daniels series is a clear improvement over the first one, with a tighter and more memorable plot. A (hot, of course)</span>
  <span id="freeText17474147930571051738" style="display:none">April 2018 update: After holding out for two years, I finally renewed my $70 nonresident library card. I was so stoked when I found that the library now has the entire Kate Daniels series! I brought The. Entire. Series. home with me, and I’m starting with this one and working my way through the series, since there are a few I’ve never read. Cheer me on!<br /><br />This second book in the Kate Daniels series is a clear improvement over the first one, with a tighter and more memorable plot. A (hot, of course) guy with teleporting powers and a mean crossbow has stolen maps from the local werepack, and Curran, the Beast Lord, and his chief of security, Jim, are determined to get them back, partly out of pride for Pack security. This leads to a 13 year old girl, Julie, who has a highly valuable ability to see and sort magic by type and color, and who also has a mad crush on Red, a juvenile delinquent with secret plans of his own. <br /><br />Kate's investigation leads her and the Pack to a looming battle for power, involving a powerful underworld figure, Morfran, the Irish war goddess Morrigan, and her magical cauldron. Also witches of various sorts and powers, including the Maiden, the Crone and the Mother. The Andrews team does a great job of incorporating obscure mythology from all over the world into their novels. <br /><br />Kate Daniels is my favorite kick-ass heroine. She's impertinent:<blockquote>The vampire stared at me, his mouth slack as Ghastek assessed his options. I took a couple of forms from my desk, put them in the vampire's mouth, and pulled them up by their edges.<br /><br />"What are you doing?" Ghastek asked.<br /><br />"My hole puncher broke."<br /><br />"You have no respect for the undead."</blockquote>And she's quick and tough as nails:<blockquote>"I tell you what, you put the maps right here on the bed. On the count of three, we each grab them. If you win, I tell you who he is. If I win, I get you. . . On three. One," he said, bending forward like a runner. "Two."<br /><br />He lunged for the maps. I grabbed the chair and hit him with it. He went down. I hit him again to make sure he stayed that way, stepped over him, and picked up the maps. "I win. Your problem is, you underestimate me because I'm a woman."</blockquote>The Kate Daniels books aren't terribly deep, but they're definitely a lot of fun, mixed with some sexual tension.<br /><br />One more thing: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The sexual tension with Curran is driving me crazy!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> In a good way. Excuse me while I go have my guy feed me something . . .</span>
  <a data-text-id="17474147930571051738" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=pnr-uf">pnr-uf</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3147418591" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10124521494590488327"><a href='https://readasaurus.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='https://www.instagram.com/alwaysbeebooked/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Instagram</a> || <a href='https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twitter</a> || <a href='https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Facebook</a> || <a href='http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon</a> || <a href='https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pinterest</a><br/><br/><br/>When I was a teenager, one of my favorite websites in the whole wide world was Quizilla. It was a magical wonderland of user-made quizzes and bad fic, where you could spend the day finding out what anime girl element you were (with ~beautiful pics~) or you could spend the day reading smutty fanfic about Louis and Lestat. Or, if you were so inclined, you could browse original fic submitted by users, often written in the second person, whe</span>
  <span id="freeText10124521494590488327" style="display:none"><a href="https://readasaurus.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/alwaysbeebooked/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> || <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a><br><br><br>When I was a teenager, one of my favorite websites in the whole wide world was Quizilla. It was a magical wonderland of user-made quizzes and bad fic, where you could spend the day finding out what anime girl element you were (with ~beautiful pics~) or you could spend the day reading smutty fanfic about Louis and Lestat. Or, if you were so inclined, you could browse original fic submitted by users, often written in the second person, where "you," the heroine, were some kind of hybrid angel-vampire-werewolf-faerie combination and had a veritable reverse-harem of male love interests to chose from, distinguishable only in the colors of their hair and the way they demonstrated their instant love for <i>you</i>.<br><br><br><br>The Kate Daniels series is leagues above the kind of trash I used to read on Quizilla (which is now sadly defunct), but it taps into that same insatiable craving for fun, addictive stories that balance action and romance. Set in a world where magic is at constant war with tech, Kate Daniels is that hybrid Mary Sue like character from my childhood-- only now she's all grown up and sporting big girl pants and a pretty intimidating sword named Slayer.<br><br><br><br>In this book, an arson case ends up leading Kate down a rabbit hole of missing witches, undead mermaids, and evil cauldrons. Every time there's a magic flare, something sinister happens, and it's dark and ancient magic. People are playing with deadly gods. Naturally, the Pack ends up being involved, and Kate clashes against the attractive werelion, Curran. But there's other attractive dudes, like the so-bad-he's-good thief, Bran, and Saiman, the seductive shape-changer. Basically every guy Kate meets in this book has some kind of interest in her, which should have been annoying-- but the way she's written, you can kind of understand why she's so magnetic. I found her compelling.<br><br><br><br>As always, the book is a little slow to start, but as soon as the action picks up, I'm questioning any doubts I ever had about this wife-and-husband writing duo. They've yet to truly disappoint me with any of their books and MAGIC BURNS was no exception. Luckily I also own books three and four, and I just checked out book five in ebook from the library, so I'm all set to binge read this series!<br><br><br><br>4 to 4.5 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="10124521494590488327" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1098850787" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8792751396734334809"><i> Reread 6/2018 </i> <br/><br/><b> 4.5 "I'm really starting to love this series" stars </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “You don't cause problems. You cause catastrophes.” </i> </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/magicburnscollage.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415391752i/11782187._SX540_.png' alt=' photo magicburnscollage.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>While investigating a mysterious bowman who killed her mark, mercenary Kate Daniels finds herself in the custody of a pre-teen girl. Turns out the young street girl has some magical powers, the kind of powers that 1 in 10,000 people get and there are creatures coming after her. Kate must go to the last person she wants help from, Curran, and together they fight to help </span>
  <span id="freeText8792751396734334809" style="display:none"><i> Reread 6/2018 </i> <br><br><b> 4.5 "I'm really starting to love this series" stars </b><br><br><b> <i> “You don't cause problems. You cause catastrophes.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/magicburnscollage.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415391752i/11782187._SX540_.png" alt=" photo magicburnscollage.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>While investigating a mysterious bowman who killed her mark, mercenary Kate Daniels finds herself in the custody of a pre-teen girl. Turns out the young street girl has some magical powers, the kind of powers that 1 in 10,000 people get and there are creatures coming after her. Kate must go to the last person she wants help from, Curran, and together they fight to help the girl. <br><br>Another great installment in this series. The plot thickens with this book but we still have some questions left unanswered. Such as:<br>-What exactly is Kate?<br>-Who is Roland?<br>-What interest does Curran have in Kate?<br><br>My favorite part of this book was the interactions between Kate and Curran. Their banter is so much fun to read and I am dying for the two of them to admit they have the hots for each other.<br><br><b> <i> “Not only will you sleep with me, but you will say 'please.'"<br>I stared at him, shocked. <br>The smile widened. "You will say 'please' before and 'thank you' after." <br>Nervous laughter bubbled up. "You've gone insane. All that peroxide in your hair finally did your brain in, Goldilocks.” </i> </b><br><br>Ilona Andrews writing duo has done it again and marked a winner in my book. The world building and character development are awesome, and that's all I ask for in urban fantasy. Well, those two things and the hopes of romance. <br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/lioj.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415391752i/11782188._SY540_.png" alt=" photo lioj.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Short review from me, because I'm dying to get to the third book. I keep hearing rumors about a hot tub scene ;-)</span>

<div id="review_723399150" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/723399150" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/723399150?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">EVERYONE!!!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=4-5-stars">4-5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=fantastic-fantasy">fantastic-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=book-boyfriend-material">book-boyfriend-material</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with">chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=adorable-alphas">adorable-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chocolate-pms-day-reads">chocolate-pms-day-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=super-sidekicks">super-sidekicks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=kick-ass-heroines">kick-ass-heroines</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer723399150" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5492207066027099600"><b>Sale Alert:</b> This is one of my favorite all time UF series and the first few books are currently on sale $1.99<br/><br/><b>Kate Daniels Buddy Read/Reread on May 11 with the gang at <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ilona Andrews Addicts (IAA)</a></b><br/><br/><b>4.5 Stars bumped up a half star from first read<br/><br/>Revisited review after Re-read on Jun 30, 2014</b><br/><br/>Ilona Andrews is an author I think I can re-read time and time again. I liked this book even more the second time around. The magic and mythology drew me in and the plot and story were even better the second time </span>
  <span id="freeText5492207066027099600" style="display:none"><b>Sale Alert:</b> This is one of my favorite all time UF series and the first few books are currently on sale $1.99<br><br><b>Kate Daniels Buddy Read/Reread on May 11 with the gang at <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa" rel="nofollow noopener">Ilona Andrews Addicts (IAA)</a></b><br><br><b>4.5 Stars bumped up a half star from first read<br><br>Revisited review after Re-read on Jun 30, 2014</b><br><br>Ilona Andrews is an author I think I can re-read time and time again. I liked this book even more the second time around. The magic and mythology drew me in and the plot and story were even better the second time around.<br><br>I got excited when new characters, which will be around throughout the series, were introduced and the chemistry building and the slow burn between Kate and Curran is even more enticing the second time around.<br><br><i>But I didn’t know what it meant!”<br>Aunt B frowned. “Doesn’t matter. You need to be very careful right now. When Curran wants something, he doesn’t become distracted. He goes after it and he doesn’t stop until he obtains his goal no matter what it takes. That tenacity is what makes him an alpha.”<br>“You’re scaring me.”<br>“Scared might be too strong a word, but in your place, I would definitely be concerned.”</i><br><br>I lapped up all Kate/Curran page time together and saw new things I missed the first time. I loved Aunt B’s very apt description of Curran and now that he has his interests set on Kate I don’t think she stands a chance of resisting for long. Again the epilogue totally pulled on every hopeless romantic heartstring I have.<br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/asyouwish_zpsac1312eb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404137669i/10196490.jpg" alt=" photo asyouwish_zpsac1312eb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Onto Magic Strikes which was one of my favorites of the series.<br><br> <br><b>Original Review Sept 24, 2013</b><br><br><br>Kate seems to have trouble follow her no matter what she does and no matter how hard she tries to avoid it trouble has her address and knocks softly at the door. In this installment the author shows us just how far the extremes of Kate’s world can swing as there is the equivalent of a typhoon of magic coming. Called a flare the ebb and flow between magic and tech become increasingly unstable and all the magical creatures are feeling the pull including Kate. It is a time when the gods come out to play and Kate needs to find a way to keep one in particular out of this world.<br><br><b><i>“You don't cause problems. An unpiloted vampire causes problems. You cause catastrophes.”</i></b><br><br>I enjoyed this plot arc more than the last. It could just be because I knew more about the world created here and could focus more on the story than in the last book or it could be because the reader get a more serious and deeper look into the woman that is Kate Daniels. Kate is a strong, independent and willful woman that can kick some serious butt. But, she is so much more than that and in this book I really was able to see the softer part of Kate, the part that motivates her to protect others and keep them at a distance. It is revealed little by a little a few pieces of her past until you are pretty sure you know where she comes from and the bigger battle she will have to face eventually. Her interactions with Julie a teenage girl she is trying to help really humanize her.<br><br><b><i>“I'm a substitute mom."<br>"You're more like a crazy aunt who only gets called when somebody needs bailing out of jail.”</i></b><br><br>The use of mythologies I’m not familiar with was also a boon to the author. She could have chosen the normal Greek, Roman or Egyptian mythologies for the deities in the story but she took some of the lore from Celtic origins that were new to me and made the story much more likable and I didn’t knit pick the mythology apart because well I just didn’t know anything about it. It fit the unusualness of the world Ilona Andrews has created.<br><br>The only thing I wanted more of in this book was Kate/Curran time together. I love the chemistry between them and the fight against the inevitable. It’s great that Kate is getting the job done and kicking butt on her own but I really look forward to the two of them having more page time together. I’m sure it’s coming and the buildup of anticipation is great but I want more now. <br>	<br><b><i>“You know what I like about you? You have no sense. You sit here in my house, you can barely hold a spoon, and you're telling me 'no'. You'd pull on Death's whiskers if you could reach them.”</i></b><br><br>My absolute favorite moment between them is on the very last page when Curran says<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[”As you wish.” I think I swooned for him right then and there and I fell in love with Ilona Andrews at the moment. How perfect to put a line from the Princess Bride into her book  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>Magic Burns is a stronger book than Magic Bites as all the main characters develop an extra layer to them. This is teaming up to be a favorite series of mine. I can’t wait to see what happens to Kate next.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="5492207066027099600" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_110522268" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/110522268" />
    <a title="carol. " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3978225-carol"><img alt="carol. " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1307934801p2/3978225.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/110522268?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="carol. " class="user" itemprop="url" name="carol. " href="/user/show/3978225-carol">carol. </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">everyone who likes fantasy and kick-butt women</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3978225-carol?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3978225-carol?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3978225-carol?shelf=female-lead">female-lead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3978225-carol?shelf=desert-island">desert-island</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3978225-carol?shelf=my-library">my-library</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3978225-carol?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3978225-carol?shelf=shifter">shifter</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer110522268" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14625803715341594890">I've procrastinated forever in writing this review. Magic Burns is one of my frequent re-reads, and I'm not sure I can do it justice. <br/><br/>What keeps drawing me back? An interesting heroine that is confident, skilled in her field, funny, occasionally lonely, caring despite herself and lives according to an ethical code? Action that builds from the somewhat ridiculous (a salamander pyromaniac) to the tragic (spikey dogs) to epic (a battle between shapeshifters and gods)? Relationship building that giv</span>
  <span id="freeText14625803715341594890" style="display:none">I've procrastinated forever in writing this review. Magic Burns is one of my frequent re-reads, and I'm not sure I can do it justice. <br /><br />What keeps drawing me back? An interesting heroine that is confident, skilled in her field, funny, occasionally lonely, caring despite herself and lives according to an ethical code? Action that builds from the somewhat ridiculous (a salamander pyromaniac) to the tragic (spikey dogs) to epic (a battle between shapeshifters and gods)? Relationship building that gives equal importance to girlfriends, adopted family and potential romance? A sophisticated vision of a post-apocalypic Atlanta that shifts from magic to tech? Vampires that are not romantacized and moreover, most empathetically, do not <i> sparkle</i>? Hard to say, but it's a favorite. If they ever release it in hardcover, I'll buy it in a flash, because my paperback is worn out.<br /><br />Kate is the heroine of the series, and one of my all-time favorite characters.<br /><br />She's anything but a sweet talking diplomat:<br /><b><br />"Negotiate. He [Jim] wanted me to engage a lunatic who had already burned four people into smoking meat. Okay, I could do that.<br />'Alright, Jeremy,' I yelled into the night. 'Give me the salamander and I won't cut your head off!'"<br /></b><br />She's got a gift of understatement:<br /><b><br />"His nose no longer looked broken. No blood, either. Wonderful. Not only could he teleport, but he also regenerated while he did it. If he started spitting fire, we'd be all set."<br /></b><br />She knows a losing battle when she sees one:<br /><b><br />"I looked at his face and saw the decisive thrust of the adolescent jaw. No intelligent life there. I turned to Julie."<br /></b><br />She's creative:<br /><b><br />"The vampire started at me, his mouth slack as Ghastek assessed his options. I took a couple of forms from my desk, put them in the vamp's mouth, and pulled them up by their edges.<br />'What are you doing?' Ghastek asked.<br />'My hole puncher broke.'<br />'You have no respect for the undead."<br /></b><br />And sometimes, very rarely, she has nothing to say:<br /><b><br />"She [Julie] shrugged. 'Sex. Red knows a ritual that would give him my powers if I do sex with him.'<br />I stared at her, speechless. There were so many things wrong with what she said that my brain experienced a momentary shutdown."<br /></b><br />But don't be misled, she isn't all sarcasm, and her confrontations with evil aren't marked by trading witticisms. But there's enough humor to ease the way in to the serious stuff. <br /><br />Five stars, again and again.<br /><br /><br />Re-read May, 2017, because my cousin was borrowing it. Idk, maybe I needed to make sure it was good or something, before I lent it to her? Or just in case she didn't return it?<br /><br /><br />Cross posted at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://clsiewert.wordpress.com/2013/04/04/magic-burns-kate-daniels-2-by-ilona-andrews-or-my-favorite-uf-heroine/">http://clsiewert.wordpress.com/2013/0...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14625803715341594890" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1209546625" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1209546625" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1209546625?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

  <i>"Rambo called, he wants his bandana back."<br/>"This Rambo, he a friend of yours?"<br/>"Who's Rambo?" Julie asked.<br/>If a cultural reference flies over a man's head, does it make a sound if nobody else gets it?</i>

</a><br/>(This is Rambo, for all of you youngsters)<br/><br/>I'm still loving Kate. As a matter of fact, I like her better in this book than the first one. She is more human, but still hilario</span>
  <span id="freeText9907320150205916300" style="display:none">Rereading this with the lovelies at the Ilona Andrews Addicts group. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464034168i/19188190.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Here's my original review from a year ago:</i><br><br>***********<br><b>
  <i>"Rambo called, he wants his bandana back."<br>"This Rambo, he a friend of yours?"<br>"Who's Rambo?" Julie asked.<br>If a cultural reference flies over a man's head, does it make a sound if nobody else gets it?</i>

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424767670i/13801118.jpg" alt="rambo photo: rambo 1171199-Rambo-Penticton.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>(This is Rambo, for all of you youngsters)<br><br>I'm still loving Kate. As a matter of fact, I like her better in this book than the first one. She is more human, but still hilarious and kickass at the same time.<br><br>In this book, we get all of these strange creatures from Celtic mythology that I have never heard of before, and that was refreshing. The monsters were strange and scary, and I liked the introduction of Julie and how she affected Kate. I love the "crazy aunt" reference to Kate's relationship to her. Derek is also becoming a great teenage werewolf side-kick.<br><br>Of course, the relationship between Kate and Curran is really fun. I especially like reading all of the reviews here and seeing all of the Chris Hemsworth gifs. Not hard on the eyes at all... Keep them coming, girls!<br><br>Since Curran's hair was longer in this book:<br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/chris%20hemsworth" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_52611663" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/52611663" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/52611663?book_show_action=true">Apr 14, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of really good action-oriented urban fantasy</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=owned-copy">owned-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-to-die-for">hero-to-die-for</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=vampire">vampire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorite-or-autobuy-author">favorite-or-autobuy-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=warrior-woman">warrior-woman</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=mythical-beasties">mythical-beasties</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=heroine-i-adore">heroine-i-adore</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer52611663" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2730150537091316303">Kate Daniels, could you be more awesome? Nope. This book rocked my world! I loved the first book, but I loved this one even more. Kate Daniels is such a cool heroine. She's not only kickbutt, independent, and snarky, but she's utterly likeable. She's down to earth, and one of those heroines I think a guy or a girl could get along with equally well. I like her quick thinking and her ability to get out of some pretty nasty spots. And her willingness to do the right thing, even at personal cost to </span>
  <span id="freeText2730150537091316303" style="display:none">Kate Daniels, could you be more awesome? Nope. This book rocked my world! I loved the first book, but I loved this one even more. Kate Daniels is such a cool heroine. She's not only kickbutt, independent, and snarky, but she's utterly likeable. She's down to earth, and one of those heroines I think a guy or a girl could get along with equally well. I like her quick thinking and her ability to get out of some pretty nasty spots. And her willingness to do the right thing, even at personal cost to herself. And she's so funny! I think her one liners are hilarious, and her internal dialogue really puts me in the action and gives me an identification factor.<br /><br />The action in this book was fantastic. A little bit gory and gruesome, but the fast pace allows you to tolerate that aspect fairly well. It's like watching a really good movie. The climax was one heck of a battle. I can't say I've read many other urban fantasy books where the conclusion had me so riveted. Ilona Andrews really knows how to write action, and that's coming from a very picky reader when it comes to action scenes.<br /><br />The use of magic and the ugly and beneficial aspects fit very well with this particular story. The descriptions of the freaky version of a modern day Atlanta that has been morphed by magic into a sort of dystopian future setting, rife with deadly and mystical creatures were very vivid and iconic. I think this is such a great idea for an urban fantasy series.<br /><br />I thought the Celtic mythology elements were very well done. The whole use of Morrigan and the Formorians. It tied in so smoothly with the overall plot. There wasn't boring periods where info dump slowed down the story. There was a huge element of risk here where you really worried if everything was going to be resolved well. <br /><br />To be honest, I didn't really think of Curran as much of a love interest in the first book. There was a bit of potential, and he had me intrigued, although I wasn't sold. But, I could really see the attraction between Kate and Curran, and I was digging Curran pretty hard. He's...well, he's the Beast Lord, with all that applies. I like the back and forth between Kate and Curran. How she's attracted and kind of scared of him (because he's pretty scary, let's face it), but she won't allow herself not to stand up to him. It's pretty clear that Curran has it bad for Kate. I loved his courtship ritual that she didn't pick up on (it had to be explained by a few members of the Pack). I love the slow build of their relationship, with all the nice 'flirting moments'. I can't way to see things progress with this couple. <br /><br />Kate's sidekicks were cool. Derek is adorable but a tough fighter. I loved Julie. I hope to see more of her. All the contacts and the acquaintances that Kate has stand out in my mind, each adding to the story in crucial ways. And then there was Bran. A very interesting character with a complex relationship with Kate. <br /><br />Man, oh, man. I had no idea how much I would come to love this series. It just keeps getting better and better. I was so pumped after reading this book, it took me a whole hour to calm down. Magic Burns is highly recommended to the discerning urban fantasy reader who likes a great heroine, kickbutt action, wonderful world-building, and intriguing secondary characters. I'm going to try to keep myself from devouring this series back to back. I need to have a guaranteed read in my pile for that 'rainy day', and the Kate Daniels series is definitely that!</span>
  <a data-text-id="2730150537091316303" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1442443801" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1442443801" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1442443801?book_show_action=true">Nov 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1442443801" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer173993282299859928"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This was hell and I was its fury.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b>Celtic mythology,witch covens,lots of ass kicking and HOT shapeshifters?</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410113062ra/11063574.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Kate Daniels is worried.A powerful wave of magic known as the flare is going to strike Atlanta and make possible for malevolent deities to walk among the humans,spreading chaos and death,and somehow in the center of the crisis is the street urchin Kate's looking after.And the world's gone mad.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I needed to find Julie,find her mom,convince a sociopath to donate some blood </i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText173993282299859928" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This was hell and I was its fury.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Celtic mythology,witch covens,lots of ass kicking and HOT shapeshifters?</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410113062ra/11063574.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kate Daniels is worried.A powerful wave of magic known as the flare is going to strike Atlanta and make possible for malevolent deities to walk among the humans,spreading chaos and death,and somehow in the center of the crisis is the street urchin Kate's looking after.And the world's gone mad.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I needed to find Julie,find her mom,convince a sociopath to donate some blood for the good of mankind,and deal with a tentacled atrocity swaddled in cloth and his rabid mermaids.I needed coffee.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1811543.Magic_Burns__Kate_Daniels___2_" title="Magic Burns (Kate Daniels, #2) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Burns</a> was <b>so.bloody.entertaining!!</b>I love Kate's narration,she's oozing <b>sarcasm</b> and her retorts are always <b>hilarious</b>!It's a book that keeps you glued to the story from the start,there's no retrieve from <b>action</b> and <b>suspense</b>!The world-building was solid,most of my questions were answered and I have to say,it's freaking <b>genious</b>!I mean of course I'd prefer to step into a giant turtle's throat than to live in magic stricken Atlanta,but I bow to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/21748.Ilona_Andrews" title="Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Ilona Andrews</a>'s <b>creativity</b> and storytelling!<b>Blood and gore and awesome battles</b>,a parade of <b>cool characters</b> (I hate to admit it but I enjoy Ghastek so much),mythical creatures (finally an author that got right <b>Greek mythology</b>) and a huge dose of <b>badassery</b> and that's it,you get obsessed!And there's also <b>Curran</b>.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Not only will you sleep with me, but you will say 'please.'”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445012961ra/16587067.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The <b>gray-eyed homicidal SEXY maniac</b> makes me <b>swoon</b>.The <b>sexual tension</b> between Kate and Curran is killing me,their <b>will-or-won't-they</b> status is a slow death.They fight and insult and infuriate and drive each other crazy but at the same time there are sparks and butterflies!And I scream at them for not seeing the obvious and I'm like<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447528542ra/17016210.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I turned around and looked at the scenery.Having a streak of drool hang from my mouth would seriously cramp my style.Besides,if he full-out flexed,I would probably faint.Or jump of the building.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Fine,fine I'll stop gushing about Curran.But I'm telling you guys,the second book was better than the first and I can't wait to read the third!It seems that <i>magic burns</i> and I'm totally fried.</span>
  <a data-text-id="173993282299859928" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14837200734326420060" style="display:none">Its as good as the first one. The only problem I have with this book is that the first 50 pages or so was so damn slow, I had to force myself through it. After that the rest was a piece of cake.<br /><br />World building✅<br />Plot✅<br />Writing ✅<br />Characters✅<br />Magic system ✅<br /><br /> This book has it all.<br />If you don't know before, know now, am a sucker for good magic system and characters.<br />We have some new characters in these but my favourites are Julie, Raphael and Bran.<br /><br />Julie is a 13 year old homeless girl with a rare magic, her mom is missing and Kate came across the girl when she was working on the case.<br /><br />Raphael is a bouda, a werehyena, he is not much different from the animal hyena, he is reckless and crazy, but according to Kate and the female boudas he is beautiful, which is a dangerous combination given the fact that he is a great fighter.<br /><br />Bran is some kind of immortal, human with long life, he works for a goddess. He is hot as hell with cool powers like teleportation and regeneration. His moral compass needs major work.<br /><br />We have the regulars, Kate, Curran, Derek, Andrea and Jim.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“You don’t cause problems. An unpiloted vampire causes problems. You cause catastrophes.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Kate is as badass as ever, what she did for Julie here blew my mind. I love that even though she is a working target, she still cares about others.<br /><br />Derek my teenage werewolf is still as cool as ever, he was barely in this, I hope that changes in the next book.<br /><br />Curran also was barely in this, he was in this for like 50% only, so not cool Ilona Andrews. The few part that we saw him he is still the same. And he is finally warming up to Kate.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13739301062099891306">Buddy-read with the amazetastic Casey to commence July 20th..... because I can't seem to read anything I am supposed to right now!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1468949274i/19763567.jpg' width='236' height='260' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>Review, such as it were....</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1470341282i/19917156._SX540_.jpg' width='372' height='209.4' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>A Kraft Dinner review of a Kate Daniels novel.</b> <br/><br/><b>3.5 Stars</b> <br/><br/>I liked <u>Magic Burns</u> a little bit better than the first one in the series. Honestly, I don’t know that it will ever match the mania I felt picking up the <i>Fever series</i> last year but I’m totally okay with that. This series is fun. It doesn’t take itself too seriously, the way the books </span>
  <span id="freeText13739301062099891306" style="display:none">Buddy-read with the amazetastic Casey to commence July 20th..... because I can't seem to read anything I am supposed to right now!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1468949274i/19763567.jpg" width="236" height="260" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Review, such as it were....</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1470341282i/19917156._SX540_.jpg" width="372" height="209.4" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>A Kraft Dinner review of a Kate Daniels novel.</b> <br><br><b>3.5 Stars</b> <br><br>I liked <u>Magic Burns</u> a little bit better than the first one in the series. Honestly, I don’t know that it will ever match the mania I felt picking up the <i>Fever series</i> last year but I’m totally okay with that. This series is fun. It doesn’t take itself too seriously, the way the books are paced and written kind of reminds me of the TV series “Charmed”. There is a mystery in the foreground that our heroine, Kate, finds herself wrapped up in and as the story unfolds towards the end of the novel we learn a little more about her and the other characters. It’s a method I find myself enjoying quite a bit, at the moment. It’s not rewriting the wheel or anything but it is definitely fun!<br><br><i>“You know what I like about you? You have no sense. You sit here in my house, you can barely hold a spoon, and you're telling me 'no'. You'd pull on Death's whiskers if you could reach them.”</i><br><br>The mystery of Kate’s past becomes a little bit more clear in this novel. We also get to watch her develop some interesting friendships and battle her feelings about Curran. Her snarky attitude is back, in a major way and I found myself laughing out loud at many of her exchanges with Curran and the others. <br><br>This time she is at the centre of a mystery involving a missing coven, a hole in the earth, gigantic metal birds and a mysterious stranger with a bow. I am definitely enjoying this series so far!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13739301062099891306" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText6437124601005853994" style="display:none">Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/5600230-armina" rel="nofollow noopener">Armina</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/17237503-eilonwy" rel="nofollow noopener">Eilonwy</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3328287-asya" rel="nofollow noopener">Asya</a>.<br /><br />Kate Daniels' occasional partner and shape-shifter Jim asks her to help him apprehend a mad arsonist. They got him, but a mysterious sniper kills the culprit right in front of their eyes. Kate starts looking for the guy and becomes tangled with a teen girl looking for her missing mom, bad-ass monsters from Celtic mythology coming to life, and magic flares which make shape-shifters struggle to keep their bestial part in check. Non-stop action ensures.<br /><br />I found the writing quality is exactly the same as in the first book. If you like that one, you will like the second one as well. Once again most of the monsters, including the Celtic ones I mentioned are of non-mainstream variety which is good and welcome. The action parts were good and we finally get some initial glimpses and hints at Kate's origins.<br /><br />My only complaint is about the Kate character herself. It seems to me she spent way too much time trying to push Curran around for no other purpose other than to see how far he can be pushed - this is at the time when the guy really had to keep a firm grip on his humanity because of the flares I mentioned above.<br /><br />Other than this minor part I really have no problems with the book and its rating is exactly the same and for the first one: <b>3.5 stars</b>. I rounded up the rating for the first book, so I round down the rating for this one to even it out. <br /><br />This review is a copy/paste of my BookLikes one: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://gene.booklikes.com/post/969517/the-writing-quality-is-exactly-on-the-same-level-as-in-the-first-book-of-the-series">http://gene.booklikes.com/post/969517...</a></span>

  <span id="freeText258462770826722049" style="display:none">I finished this last night just before sleeping, so of course Kate followed me into my dreams. <br /> The last battle was so visual and I kept seeing her running in with both swords flying.   <i>
    <b>"You have the Pack. You're surrounded by people who would fall over themselves for the pleasure of your company. I have no one. My parents are dead, my entire family is gone. I have no friends. Except Jim, and that's more of a working relationship than anything else. I have no lover. I can't even have a pet, because I'm not at the house often enough to keep it from starving. When I come crawling home, bleeding and filthy and exhausted, the house is dark and empty. Nobody keeps the porch light on for me. Nobody hugs me and says, 'Hey, I'm glad you made it. I'm glad you're okay. I was worried.' Nobody cares if I live or die. Nobody makes me coffee, nobody holds me before I go to bed, nobody fixes my medicine when I'm sick. I'm by myself."</b>
  </i>

  <span id="freeText10140865636594931216" style="display:none">In this second book of the series, Kate is still tough, brave, unpretentious, sassy, humane and loyal. Can you tell that she is my current favourite paranormal heroine? :-)<br />I loved the world building in the first book, where we got introduced to this strange reality where technology and magic alternate. Here we see that magic is gaining ground and sooner or later all vestiges of our world ( e.g. cars) will disappear. Magic flows and pulsates through the book and all the supernatural creatures( shape shifters, vampire masters, witches) have to find their own ways to control themselves.<br />Magic flare is also a special time when gods and goddesses can come to life and manifest themselves on earth. The plot focuses on Celtic mythology and there are new monsters to fight- reeves.<br />Kate makes new friends and saves a teenage girl Julie who becomes a sort of a charge for her. We also get more hints about Kate's powers and her origin.<br />I'm not a big fan of insta love, so I am happy with the slow development of Kate and Curran's relationship. They are still two of a kind:-)<br />Now I am ready for book 3.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11097203845609779483"><b>4 STARS!!</b><br/><br/><b>Magic Burns</b> is the 2nd book in the <i>Kate Daniels</i> urban fantasy series. I really liked this much more then the 1st book in the series. It just goes to show that it pays to stick with a series until you have an idea of the world building and characters. <b>Magic Burns</b> was better written and the characters had better dialogue and attitude.<br/>The magic in this is also better understood and I loved all the references to Celt goddesses and gods along with the Druid information. Fun stuff to read!<br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(vi</a></span>
  <span id="freeText11097203845609779483" style="display:none"><b>4 STARS!!</b><br /><br /><b>Magic Burns</b> is the 2nd book in the <i>Kate Daniels</i> urban fantasy series. I really liked this much more then the 1st book in the series. It just goes to show that it pays to stick with a series until you have an idea of the world building and characters. <b>Magic Burns</b> was better written and the characters had better dialogue and attitude.<br />The magic in this is also better understood and I loved all the references to Celt goddesses and gods along with the Druid information. She's tough, a badass, holds her own against the alpha men and is still funny!<br /><br />I'm definitely continuing with the series because I need to find out who <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Kate really is and what her magic powers are!
